Top Modern Decklists: M-R
=========================



 Posted in [COVERAGE ARCHIVE](/en/events/coverage)
 on February 8, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











 These players earned 18 match points (went 6-4) in the Modern Constructed portion of Pro Tour *Fate Reforged*. Want to see what they played? Check our their decklists below!
